2025-08-05 23:57:11.481 +03:00 [INF] Executed DbCommand (105ms) [Parameters=[@__ToLower_0='?' (Size = 50)], CommandType='"Text"', CommandTimeout='30']
SELECT DISTINCT [g2].[Access], [g2].[CanDelete], [g2].[CanInsert], [g2].[CanUpdate], [m0].[IconClass], [g2].[MenuID] AS [MenuId], [m0].[Name], [m0].[Path], [m0].[ParentID] AS [MenuParentId], [u].[Username]
FROM [Users] AS [u]
INNER JOIN (
    SELECT [u0].[UserId], [u0].[GroupId]
    FROM [UserGroups] AS [u0]
    WHERE [u0].[IsDeleted] = CAST(0 AS bit)

SELECT DISTINCT [g2].[Access], [g2].[CanDelete], [g2].[CanInsert], [g2].[CanUpdate], [m0].[IconClass], [g2].[MenuID] AS [MenuId], [m0].[Name], [m0].[Path], [m0].[ParentID] AS [MenuParentId], [u].[Username]

    SELECT [u0].[UserId], [u0].[GroupId]
    FROM [UserGroups] AS [u0]
    WHERE [u0].[IsDeleted] = CAST(0 AS bit)
) AS [u1] ON [u].[id] = [u1].[UserId]

    SELECT [g].[id]
    FROM [Groups] AS [g]
    WHERE [g].[IsDeleted] = CAST(0 AS bit)
) AS [g0] ON [u1].[GroupId] = [g0].[id]

    SELECT [g1].[GroupID], [g1].[MenuID], [g1].[Access], [g1].[CanDelete], [g1].[CanInsert], [g1].[CanUpdate]
    FROM [GroupsMenus] AS [g1]
    WHERE [g1].[IsDeleted] = CAST(0 AS bit)
) AS [g2] ON [g0].[id] = [g2].[GroupID]

) AS [m0] ON [g2].[MenuID] = [m0].[id]
